00718 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(PyObject *o, PyObject* j) {
00719     PyObject *r;
00720     if (!j) return NULL;
00721     r = PyObject_GetItem(o, j);
00722     Py_DECREF(j);
00723     return r;
00724 }
00725 
00726 
00727 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt_List(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00728                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_List_Fast(o, i) : \
00729                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00730 
00731 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_List_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00732     if (likely(o != Py_None)) {
00733         if (likely((0 <= i) & (i < PyList_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00734             PyObject *r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00735             Py_INCREF(r);
00736             return r;
00737         }
00738         else if ((-PyList_GET_SIZE(o) <= i) & (i < 0)) {
00739             PyObject *r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, PyList_GET_SIZE(o) + i);
00740             Py_INCREF(r);
00741             return r;
00742         }
00743     }
00744     return __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00745 }
00746 
00747 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00748                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple_Fast(o, i) : \
00749                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00750 
00751 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Tuple_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00752     if (likely(o != Py_None)) {
00753         if (likely((0 <= i) & (i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00754             PyObject *r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00755             Py_INCREF(r);
00756             return r;
00757         }
00758         else if ((-PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o) <= i) & (i < 0)) {
00759             PyObject *r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o) + i);
00760             Py_INCREF(r);
00761             return r;
00762         }
00763     }
00764     return __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00765 }
00766 
00767 
00768 #define __Pyx_GetItemInt(o, i, size, to_py_func) (((size) <= sizeof(Py_ssize_t)) ? \
00769                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Fast(o, i) : \
00770                                                     __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, to_py_func(i)))
00771 
00772 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject *__Pyx_GetItemInt_Fast(PyObject *o, Py_ssize_t i) {
00773     PyObject *r;
00774     if (PyList_CheckExact(o) && ((0 <= i) & (i < PyList_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00775         r = PyList_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00776         Py_INCREF(r);
00777     }
00778     else if (PyTuple_CheckExact(o) && ((0 <= i) & (i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(o)))) {
00779         r = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(o, i);
00780         Py_INCREF(r);
00781     }
00782     else if (Py_TYPE(o)->tp_as_sequence && Py_TYPE(o)->tp_as_sequence->sq_item && (likely(i >= 0))) {
00783         r = PySequence_GetItem(o, i);
00784     }
00785     else {
00786         r = __Pyx_GetItemInt_Generic(o, PyInt_FromSsize_t(i));
00787     }
00788     return r;
00789 }

05162 static PyObject *__Pyx_GetName(PyObject *dict, PyObject *name) {
05163     PyObject *result;
05164     result = PyObject_GetAttr(dict, name);
05165     if (!result) {
05166         if (dict != __pyx_b) {
05167             PyErr_Clear();
05168             result = PyObject_GetAttr(__pyx_b, name);
05169         }
05170         if (!result) {
05171             PyErr_SetObject(PyExc_NameError, name);
05172         }
05173     }
05174     return result;
05175 }
05176 
05177 static void __Pyx_RaiseArgtupleInvalid(
05178     const char* func_name,
05179     int exact,
05180     Py_ssize_t num_min,
05181     Py_ssize_t num_max,
05182     Py_ssize_t num_found)
05183 {
05184     Py_ssize_t num_expected;
05185     const char *more_or_less;
05186 
05187     if (num_found < num_min) {
05188         num_expected = num_min;
05189         more_or_less = "at least";
05190     } else {
05191         num_expected = num_max;
05192         more_or_less = "at most";
05193     }
05194     if (exact) {
05195         more_or_less = "exactly";
05196     }
05197     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05198                  "%s() takes %s %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d positional argument%s (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d given)",
05199                  func_name, more_or_less, num_expected,
05200                  (num_expected == 1) ? "" : "s", num_found);
05201 }
05202 
05203 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_CheckKeywordStrings(
05204     PyObject *kwdict,
05205     const char* function_name,
05206     int kw_allowed)
05207 {
05208     PyObject* key = 0;
05209     Py_ssize_t pos = 0;
05210     while (PyDict_Next(kwdict, &pos, &key, 0)) {
05211         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05212         if (unlikely(!PyString_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyString_Check(key)))
05213         #else
05214         if (unlikely(!PyUnicode_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyUnicode_Check(key)))
05215         #endif
05216             goto invalid_keyword_type;
05217     }
05218     if ((!kw_allowed) && unlikely(key))
05219         goto invalid_keyword;
05220     return 1;
05221 invalid_keyword_type:
05222     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05223         "%s() keywords must be strings", function_name);
05224     return 0;
05225 invalid_keyword:
05226     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05227     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05228         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%s'",
05229         function_name, PyString_AsString(key));
05230     #else
05231         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%U'",
05232         function_name, key);
05233     #endif
05234     return 0;
05235 }
05236 
05237 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_TypeTest(PyObject *obj, PyTypeObject *type) {
05238     if (unlikely(!type)) {
05239         PyErr_Format(PyExc_SystemError, "Missing type object");
05240         return 0;
05241     }
05242     if (likely(PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, type)))
05243         return 1;
05244     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError, "Cannot convert %.200s to %.200s",
05245                  Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_name, type->tp_name);
05246     return 0;
05247 }
05248 
05249 static void __Pyx_RaiseDoubleKeywordsError(
05250     const char* func_name,
05251     PyObject* kw_name)
05252 {
05253     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05254         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
05255         "%s() got multiple values for keyword argument '%U'", func_name, kw_name);
05256         #else
05257         "%s() got multiple values for keyword argument '%s'", func_name,
05258         PyString_AS_STRING(kw_name));
05259         #endif
05260 }
05261 
05262 static int __Pyx_ParseOptionalKeywords(
05263     PyObject *kwds,
05264     PyObject **argnames[],
05265     PyObject *kwds2,
05266     PyObject *values[],
05267     Py_ssize_t num_pos_args,
05268     const char* function_name)
05269 {
05270     PyObject *key = 0, *value = 0;
05271     Py_ssize_t pos = 0;
05272     PyObject*** name;
05273     PyObject*** first_kw_arg = argnames + num_pos_args;
05274 
05275     while (PyDict_Next(kwds, &pos, &key, &value)) {
05276         name = first_kw_arg;
05277         while (*name && (**name != key)) name++;
05278         if (*name) {
05279             values[name-argnames] = value;
05280         } else {
05281             #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05282             if (unlikely(!PyString_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyString_Check(key))) {
05283             #else
05284             if (unlikely(!PyUnicode_CheckExact(key)) && unlikely(!PyUnicode_Check(key))) {
05285             #endif
05286                 goto invalid_keyword_type;
05287             } else {
05288                 for (name = first_kw_arg; *name; name++) {
05289                     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
05290                     if (PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(key) &&
05291                         PyUnicode_Compare(**name, key) == 0) break;
05292                     #else
05293                     if (PyString_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyString_GET_SIZE(key) &&
05294                         _PyString_Eq(**name, key)) break;
05295                     #endif
05296                 }
05297                 if (*name) {
05298                     values[name-argnames] = value;
05299                 } else {
05300                     /* unexpected keyword found */
05301                     for (name=argnames; name != first_kw_arg; name++) {
05302                         if (**name == key) goto arg_passed_twice;
05303                         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
05304                         if (PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyUnicode_GET_SIZE(key) &&
05305                             PyUnicode_Compare(**name, key) == 0) goto arg_passed_twice;
05306                         #else
05307                         if (PyString_GET_SIZE(**name) == PyString_GET_SIZE(key) &&
05308                             _PyString_Eq(**name, key)) goto arg_passed_twice;
05309                         #endif
05310                     }
05311                     if (kwds2) {
05312                         if (unlikely(PyDict_SetItem(kwds2, key, value))) goto bad;
05313                     } else {
05314                         goto invalid_keyword;
05315                     }
05316                 }
05317             }
05318         }
05319     }
05320     return 0;
05321 arg_passed_twice:
05322     __Pyx_RaiseDoubleKeywordsError(function_name, **name);
05323     goto bad;
05324 invalid_keyword_type:
05325     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05326         "%s() keywords must be strings", function_name);
05327     goto bad;
05328 invalid_keyword:
05329     PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
05330     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05331         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%s'",
05332         function_name, PyString_AsString(key));
05333     #else
05334         "%s() got an unexpected keyword argument '%U'",
05335         function_name, key);
05336     #endif
05337 bad:
05338     return -1;
05339 }

05341 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_IsLittleEndian(void) {
05342   unsigned int n = 1;
05343   return *(unsigned char*)(&n) != 0;
05344 }
05345 
05346 typedef struct {
05347   __Pyx_StructField root;
05348   __Pyx_BufFmt_StackElem* head;
05349   size_t fmt_offset;
05350   size_t new_count, enc_count;
05351   int is_complex;
05352   char enc_type;
05353   char new_packmode;
05354   char enc_packmode;
05355 } __Pyx_BufFmt_Context;
05356 
05357 static void __Pyx_BufFmt_Init(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx,
05358                               __Pyx_BufFmt_StackElem* stack,
05359                               __Pyx_TypeInfo* type) {
05360   stack[0].field = &ctx->root;
05361   stack[0].parent_offset = 0;
05362   ctx->root.type = type;
05363   ctx->root.name = "buffer dtype";
05364   ctx->root.offset = 0;
05365   ctx->head = stack;
05366   ctx->head->field = &ctx->root;
05367   ctx->fmt_offset = 0;
05368   ctx->head->parent_offset = 0;
05369   ctx->new_packmode = '@';
05370   ctx->enc_packmode = '@';
05371   ctx->new_count = 1;
05372   ctx->enc_count = 0;
05373   ctx->enc_type = 0;
05374   ctx->is_complex = 0;
05375   while (type->typegroup == 'S') {
05376     ++ctx->head;
05377     ctx->head->field = type->fields;
05378     ctx->head->parent_offset = 0;
05379     type = type->fields->type;
05380   }
05381 }
05382 
05383 static int __Pyx_BufFmt_ParseNumber(const char** ts) {
05384     int count;
05385     const char* t = *ts;
05386     if (*t < '0' || *t > '9') {
05387       return -1;
05388     } else {
05389         count = *t++ - '0';
05390         while (*t >= '0' && *t < '9') {
05391             count *= 10;
05392             count += *t++ - '0';
05393         }
05394     }
05395     *ts = t;
05396     return count;
05397 }
05398 
05399 static void __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(char ch) {
05400   PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05401                "Unexpected format string character: '%c'", ch);
05402 }
05403 
05404 static const char* __Pyx_BufFmt_DescribeTypeChar(char ch, int is_complex) {
05405   switch (ch) {
05406     case 'b': return "'char'";
05407     case 'B': return "'unsigned char'";
05408     case 'h': return "'short'";
05409     case 'H': return "'unsigned short'";
05410     case 'i': return "'int'";
05411     case 'I': return "'unsigned int'";
05412     case 'l': return "'long'";
05413     case 'L': return "'unsigned long'";
05414     case 'q': return "'long long'";
05415     case 'Q': return "'unsigned long long'";
05416     case 'f': return (is_complex ? "'complex float'" : "'float'");
05417     case 'd': return (is_complex ? "'complex double'" : "'double'");
05418     case 'g': return (is_complex ? "'complex long double'" : "'long double'");
05419     case 'T': return "a struct";
05420     case 'O': return "Python object";
05421     case 'P': return "a pointer";
05422     case 0: return "end";
05423     default: return "unparseable format string";
05424   }
05425 }
05426 
05427 static size_t __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToStandardSize(char ch, int is_complex) {
05428   switch (ch) {
05429     case '?': case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': return 1;
05430     case 'h': case 'H': return 2;
05431     case 'i': case 'I': case 'l': case 'L': return 4;
05432     case 'q': case 'Q': return 8;
05433     case 'f': return (is_complex ? 8 : 4);
05434     case 'd': return (is_complex ? 16 : 8);
05435     case 'g': {
05436       PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Python does not define a standard format string size for long double ('g')..");
05437       return 0;
05438     }
05439     case 'O': case 'P': return sizeof(void*);
05440     default:
05441       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
05442       return 0;
05443     }
05444 }
05445 
05446 static size_t __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToNativeSize(char ch, int is_complex) {
05447   switch (ch) {
05448     case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': return 1;
05449     case 'h': case 'H': return sizeof(short);
05450     case 'i': case 'I': return sizeof(int);
05451     case 'l': case 'L': return sizeof(long);
05452     #ifdef HAVE_LONG_LONG
05453     case 'q': case 'Q': return sizeof(PY_LONG_LONG);
05454     #endif
05455     case 'f': return sizeof(float) * (is_complex ? 2 : 1);
05456     case 'd': return sizeof(double) * (is_complex ? 2 : 1);
05457     case 'g': return sizeof(long double) * (is_complex ? 2 : 1);
05458     case 'O': case 'P': return sizeof(void*);
05459     default: {
05460       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
05461       return 0;
05462     }
05463   }
05464 }
05465 
05466 typedef struct { char c; short x; } __Pyx_st_short;
05467 typedef struct { char c; int x; } __Pyx_st_int;
05468 typedef struct { char c; long x; } __Pyx_st_long;
05469 typedef struct { char c; float x; } __Pyx_st_float;
05470 typedef struct { char c; double x; } __Pyx_st_double;
05471 typedef struct { char c; long double x; } __Pyx_st_longdouble;
05472 typedef struct { char c; void *x; } __Pyx_st_void_p;
05473 #ifdef HAVE_LONG_LONG
05474 typedef struct { char c; PY_LONG_LONG x; } __Pyx_st_longlong;
05475 #endif
05476 
05477 static size_t __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToAlignment(char ch, int is_complex) {
05478   switch (ch) {
05479     case '?': case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': return 1;
05480     case 'h': case 'H': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_short) - sizeof(short);
05481     case 'i': case 'I': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_int) - sizeof(int);
05482     case 'l': case 'L': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_long) - sizeof(long);
05483 #ifdef HAVE_LONG_LONG
05484     case 'q': case 'Q': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_longlong) - sizeof(PY_LONG_LONG);
05485 #endif
05486     case 'f': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_float) - sizeof(float);
05487     case 'd': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_double) - sizeof(double);
05488     case 'g': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_longdouble) - sizeof(long double);
05489     case 'P': case 'O': return sizeof(__Pyx_st_void_p) - sizeof(void*);
05490     default:
05491       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
05492       return 0;
05493     }
05494 }
05495 
05496 static char __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToGroup(char ch, int is_complex) {
05497   switch (ch) {
05498     case 'c': case 'b': case 'h': case 'i': case 'l': case 'q': return 'I';
05499     case 'B': case 'H': case 'I': case 'L': case 'Q': return 'U';
05500     case 'f': case 'd': case 'g': return (is_complex ? 'C' : 'R');
05501     case 'O': return 'O';
05502     case 'P': return 'P';
05503     default: {
05504       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar(ch);
05505       return 0;
05506     }
05507   }
05508 }
05509 
05510 static void __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx) {
05511   if (ctx->head == NULL || ctx->head->field == &ctx->root) {
05512     const char* expected;
05513     const char* quote;
05514     if (ctx->head == NULL) {
05515       expected = "end";
05516       quote = "";
05517     } else {
05518       expected = ctx->head->field->type->name;
05519       quote = "'";
05520     }
05521     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05522                  "Buffer dtype mismatch, expected %s%s%s but got %s",
05523                  quote, expected, quote,
05524                  __Pyx_BufFmt_DescribeTypeChar(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex));
05525   } else {
05526     __Pyx_StructField* field = ctx->head->field;
05527     __Pyx_StructField* parent = (ctx->head - 1)->field;
05528     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05529                  "Buffer dtype mismatch, expected '%s' but got %s in '%s.%s'",
05530                  field->type->name, __Pyx_BufFmt_DescribeTypeChar(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex),
05531                  parent->type->name, field->name);
05532   }
05533 }
05534 
05535 static int __Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx) {
05536   char group;
05537   size_t size, offset;
05538   if (ctx->enc_type == 0) return 0;
05539   group = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToGroup(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
05540   do {
05541     __Pyx_StructField* field = ctx->head->field;
05542     __Pyx_TypeInfo* type = field->type;
05543 
05544     if (ctx->enc_packmode == '@' || ctx->enc_packmode == '^') {
05545       size = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToNativeSize(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
05546     } else {
05547       size = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToStandardSize(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
05548     }
05549     if (ctx->enc_packmode == '@') {
05550       size_t align_at = __Pyx_BufFmt_TypeCharToAlignment(ctx->enc_type, ctx->is_complex);
05551       size_t align_mod_offset;
05552       if (align_at == 0) return -1;
05553       align_mod_offset = ctx->fmt_offset % align_at;
05554       if (align_mod_offset > 0) ctx->fmt_offset += align_at - align_mod_offset;
05555     }
05556 
05557     if (type->size != size || type->typegroup != group) {
05558       if (type->typegroup == 'C' && type->fields != NULL) {
05559         /* special case -- treat as struct rather than complex number */
05560         size_t parent_offset = ctx->head->parent_offset + field->offset;
05561         ++ctx->head;
05562         ctx->head->field = type->fields;
05563         ctx->head->parent_offset = parent_offset;
05564         continue;
05565       }
05566 
05567       __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
05568       return -1;
05569     }
05570 
05571     offset = ctx->head->parent_offset + field->offset;
05572     if (ctx->fmt_offset != offset) {
05573       PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05574                    "Buffer dtype mismatch; next field is at offset %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d but %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d expected",
05575                    (Py_ssize_t)ctx->fmt_offset, (Py_ssize_t)offset);
05576       return -1;
05577     }
05578 
05579     ctx->fmt_offset += size;
05580 
05581     --ctx->enc_count; /* Consume from buffer string */
05582 
05583     /* Done checking, move to next field, pushing or popping struct stack if needed */
05584     while (1) {
05585       if (field == &ctx->root) {
05586         ctx->head = NULL;
05587         if (ctx->enc_count != 0) {
05588           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
05589           return -1;
05590         }
05591         break; /* breaks both loops as ctx->enc_count == 0 */
05592       }
05593       ctx->head->field = ++field;
05594       if (field->type == NULL) {
05595         --ctx->head;
05596         field = ctx->head->field;
05597         continue;
05598       } else if (field->type->typegroup == 'S') {
05599         size_t parent_offset = ctx->head->parent_offset + field->offset;
05600         if (field->type->fields->type == NULL) continue; /* empty struct */
05601         field = field->type->fields;
05602         ++ctx->head;
05603         ctx->head->field = field;
05604         ctx->head->parent_offset = parent_offset;
05605         break;
05606       } else {
05607         break;
05608       }
05609     }
05610   } while (ctx->enc_count);
05611   ctx->enc_type = 0;
05612   ctx->is_complex = 0;
05613   return 0;
05614 }
05615 
05616 static const char* __Pyx_BufFmt_CheckString(__Pyx_BufFmt_Context* ctx, const char* ts) {
05617   int got_Z = 0;
05618   while (1) {
05619     switch(*ts) {
05620       case 0:
05621         if (ctx->enc_type != 0 && ctx->head == NULL) {
05622           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
05623           return NULL;
05624         }
05625         if (__Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(ctx) == -1) return NULL;
05626         if (ctx->head != NULL) {
05627           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseExpected(ctx);
05628           return NULL;
05629         }
05630         return ts;
05631       case ' ':
05632       case 10:
05633       case 13:
05634         ++ts;
05635         break;
05636       case '<':
05637         if (!__Pyx_IsLittleEndian()) {
05638           PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Little-endian buffer not supported on big-endian compiler");
05639           return NULL;
05640         }
05641         ctx->new_packmode = '=';
05642         ++ts;
05643         break;
05644       case '>':
05645       case '!':
05646         if (__Pyx_IsLittleEndian()) {
05647           PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Big-endian buffer not supported on little-endian compiler");
05648           return NULL;
05649         }
05650         ctx->new_packmode = '=';
05651         ++ts;
05652         break;
05653       case '=':
05654       case '@':
05655       case '^':
05656         ctx->new_packmode = *ts++;
05657         break;
05658       case 'T': /* substruct */
05659         {
05660           const char* ts_after_sub;
05661           size_t i, struct_count = ctx->new_count;
05662           ctx->new_count = 1;
05663           ++ts;
05664           if (*ts != '{') {
05665             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_ValueError, "Buffer acquisition: Expected '{' after 'T'");
05666             return NULL;
05667           }
05668           ++ts;
05669           ts_after_sub = ts;
05670           for (i = 0; i != struct_count; ++i) {
05671             ts_after_sub = __Pyx_BufFmt_CheckString(ctx, ts);
05672             if (!ts_after_sub) return NULL;
05673           }
05674           ts = ts_after_sub;
05675         }
05676         break;
05677       case '}': /* end of substruct; either repeat or move on */
05678         ++ts;
05679         return ts;
05680       case 'x':
05681         if (__Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(ctx) == -1) return NULL;
05682         ctx->fmt_offset += ctx->new_count;
05683         ctx->new_count = 1;
05684         ctx->enc_count = 0;
05685         ctx->enc_type = 0;
05686         ctx->enc_packmode = ctx->new_packmode;
05687         ++ts;
05688         break;
05689       case 'Z':
05690         got_Z = 1;
05691         ++ts;
05692         if (*ts != 'f' && *ts != 'd' && *ts != 'g') {
05693           __Pyx_BufFmt_RaiseUnexpectedChar('Z');
05694           return NULL;
05695         }        /* fall through */
05696       case 'c': case 'b': case 'B': case 'h': case 'H': case 'i': case 'I':
05697       case 'l': case 'L': case 'q': case 'Q':
05698       case 'f': case 'd': case 'g':
05699       case 'O':
05700         if (ctx->enc_type == *ts && got_Z == ctx->is_complex &&
05701             ctx->enc_packmode == ctx->new_packmode) {
05702           /* Continue pooling same type */
05703           ctx->enc_count += ctx->new_count;
05704         } else {
05705           /* New type */
05706           if (__Pyx_BufFmt_ProcessTypeChunk(ctx) == -1) return NULL;
05707           ctx->enc_count = ctx->new_count;
05708           ctx->enc_packmode = ctx->new_packmode;
05709           ctx->enc_type = *ts;
05710           ctx->is_complex = got_Z;
05711         }
05712         ++ts;
05713         ctx->new_count = 1;
05714         got_Z = 0;
05715         break;
05716       case ':':
05717         ++ts;
05718         while(*ts != ':') ++ts;
05719         ++ts;
05720         break;
05721       default:
05722         {
05723           int number = __Pyx_BufFmt_ParseNumber(&ts);
05724           if (number == -1) { /* First char was not a digit */
05725             PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05726                          "Does not understand character buffer dtype format string ('%c')", *ts);
05727             return NULL;
05728           }
05729           ctx->new_count = (size_t)number; 
05730         }
05731     }
05732   }
05733 }
05734 
05735 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ZeroBuffer(Py_buffer* buf) {
05736   buf->buf = NULL;
05737   buf->obj = NULL;
05738   buf->strides = __Pyx_zeros;
05739   buf->shape = __Pyx_zeros;
05740   buf->suboffsets = __Pyx_minusones;
05741 }
05742 
05743 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_GetBufferAndValidate(Py_buffer* buf, PyObject* obj, __Pyx_TypeInfo* dtype, int flags, int nd, int cast, __Pyx_BufFmt_StackElem* stack) {
05744   if (obj == Py_None || obj == NULL) {
05745     __Pyx_ZeroBuffer(buf);
05746     return 0;
05747   }
05748   buf->buf = NULL;
05749   if (__Pyx_GetBuffer(obj, buf, flags) == -1) goto fail;
05750   if (buf->ndim != nd) {
05751     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05752                  "Buffer has wrong number of dimensions (expected %d, got %d)",
05753                  nd, buf->ndim);
05754     goto fail;
05755   }
05756   if (!cast) {
05757     __Pyx_BufFmt_Context ctx;
05758     __Pyx_BufFmt_Init(&ctx, stack, dtype);
05759     if (!__Pyx_BufFmt_CheckString(&ctx, buf->format)) goto fail;
05760   }
05761   if ((unsigned)buf->itemsize != dtype->size) {
05762     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05763       "Item size of buffer (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d byte%s) does not match size of '%s' (%"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d byte%s)",
05764       buf->itemsize, (buf->itemsize > 1) ? "s" : "",
05765       dtype->name, (Py_ssize_t)dtype->size, (dtype->size > 1) ? "s" : "");
05766     goto fail;
05767   }
05768   if (buf->suboffsets == NULL) buf->suboffsets = __Pyx_minusones;
05769   return 0;
05770 fail:;
05771   __Pyx_ZeroBuffer(buf);
05772   return -1;
05773 }
05774 
05775 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_SafeReleaseBuffer(Py_buffer* info) {
05776   if (info->buf == NULL) return;
05777   if (info->suboffsets == __Pyx_minusones) info->suboffsets = NULL;
05778   __Pyx_ReleaseBuffer(info);
05779 }
05780 
05781 static void __Pyx_RaiseBufferFallbackError(void) {
05782   PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05783      "Buffer acquisition failed on assignment; and then reacquiring the old buffer failed too!");
05784 }
05785 
05786 
05787 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ErrRestore(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb) {
05788     PyObject *tmp_type, *tmp_value, *tmp_tb;
05789     PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
05790 
05791     tmp_type = tstate->curexc_type;
05792     tmp_value = tstate->curexc_value;
05793     tmp_tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
05794     tstate->curexc_type = type;
05795     tstate->curexc_value = value;
05796     tstate->curexc_traceback = tb;
05797     Py_XDECREF(tmp_type);
05798     Py_XDECREF(tmp_value);
05799     Py_XDECREF(tmp_tb);
05800 }
05801 
05802 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_ErrFetch(PyObject **type, PyObject **value, PyObject **tb) {
05803     PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
05804     *type = tstate->curexc_type;
05805     *value = tstate->curexc_value;
05806     *tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
05807 
05808     tstate->curexc_type = 0;
05809     tstate->curexc_value = 0;
05810     tstate->curexc_traceback = 0;
05811 }
05812 
05813 
05814 
05815 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05816 static void __Pyx_Raise(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb, PyObject *cause) {
05817     /* cause is unused */
05818     Py_XINCREF(type);
05819     Py_XINCREF(value);
05820     Py_XINCREF(tb);
05821     /* First, check the traceback argument, replacing None with NULL. */
05822     if (tb == Py_None) {
05823         Py_DECREF(tb);
05824         tb = 0;
05825     }
05826     else if (tb != NULL && !PyTraceBack_Check(tb)) {
05827         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05828             "raise: arg 3 must be a traceback or None");
05829         goto raise_error;
05830     }
05831     /* Next, replace a missing value with None */
05832     if (value == NULL) {
05833         value = Py_None;
05834         Py_INCREF(value);
05835     }
05836     #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
05837     if (!PyClass_Check(type))
05838     #else
05839     if (!PyType_Check(type))
05840     #endif
05841     {
05842         /* Raising an instance.  The value should be a dummy. */
05843         if (value != Py_None) {
05844             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05845                 "instance exception may not have a separate value");
05846             goto raise_error;
05847         }
05848         /* Normalize to raise <class>, <instance> */
05849         Py_DECREF(value);
05850         value = type;
05851         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
05852             if (PyInstance_Check(type)) {
05853                 type = (PyObject*) ((PyInstanceObject*)type)->in_class;
05854                 Py_INCREF(type);
05855             }
05856             else {
05857                 type = 0;
05858                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05859                     "raise: exception must be an old-style class or instance");
05860                 goto raise_error;
05861             }
05862         #else
05863             type = (PyObject*) Py_TYPE(type);
05864             Py_INCREF(type);
05865             if (!PyType_IsSubtype((PyTypeObject *)type, (PyTypeObject *)PyExc_BaseException)) {
05866                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05867                     "raise: exception class must be a subclass of BaseException");
05868                 goto raise_error;
05869             }
05870         #endif
05871     }
05872 
05873     __Pyx_ErrRestore(type, value, tb);
05874     return;
05875 raise_error:
05876     Py_XDECREF(value);
05877     Py_XDECREF(type);
05878     Py_XDECREF(tb);
05879     return;
05880 }
05881 
05882 #else /* Python 3+ */
05883 
05884 static void __Pyx_Raise(PyObject *type, PyObject *value, PyObject *tb, PyObject *cause) {
05885     if (tb == Py_None) {
05886         tb = 0;
05887     } else if (tb && !PyTraceBack_Check(tb)) {
05888         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05889             "raise: arg 3 must be a traceback or None");
05890         goto bad;
05891     }
05892     if (value == Py_None)
05893         value = 0;
05894 
05895     if (PyExceptionInstance_Check(type)) {
05896         if (value) {
05897             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05898                 "instance exception may not have a separate value");
05899             goto bad;
05900         }
05901         value = type;
05902         type = (PyObject*) Py_TYPE(value);
05903     } else if (!PyExceptionClass_Check(type)) {
05904         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05905             "raise: exception class must be a subclass of BaseException");
05906         goto bad;
05907     }
05908 
05909     if (cause) {
05910         PyObject *fixed_cause;
05911         if (PyExceptionClass_Check(cause)) {
05912             fixed_cause = PyObject_CallObject(cause, NULL);
05913             if (fixed_cause == NULL)
05914                 goto bad;
05915         }
05916         else if (PyExceptionInstance_Check(cause)) {
05917             fixed_cause = cause;
05918             Py_INCREF(fixed_cause);
05919         }
05920         else {
05921             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
05922                             "exception causes must derive from "
05923                             "BaseException");
05924             goto bad;
05925         }
05926         if (!value) {
05927             value = PyObject_CallObject(type, NULL);
05928         }
05929         PyException_SetCause(value, fixed_cause);
05930     }
05931 
05932     PyErr_SetObject(type, value);
05933 
05934     if (tb) {
05935         PyThreadState *tstate = PyThreadState_GET();
05936         PyObject* tmp_tb = tstate->curexc_traceback;
05937         if (tb != tmp_tb) {
05938             Py_INCREF(tb);
05939             tstate->curexc_traceback = tb;
05940             Py_XDECREF(tmp_tb);
05941         }
05942     }
05943 
05944 bad:
05945     return;
05946 }
05947 #endif
05948 
05949 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseNeedMoreValuesError(Py_ssize_t index) {
05950     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05951                  "need more than %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d value%s to unpack",
05952                  index, (index == 1) ? "" : "s");
05953 }
05954 
05955 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(Py_ssize_t expected) {
05956     PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
05957                  "too many values to unpack (expected %"PY_FORMAT_SIZE_T"d)", expected);
05958 }
05959 
05960 static CYTHON_INLINE void __Pyx_RaiseNoneNotIterableError(void) {
05961     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError, "'NoneType' object is not iterable");
05962 }
05963 
05964 static void __Pyx_UnpackTupleError(PyObject *t, Py_ssize_t index) {
05965     if (t == Py_None) {
05966       __Pyx_RaiseNoneNotIterableError();
05967     } else if (PyTuple_GET_SIZE(t) < index) {
05968       __Pyx_RaiseNeedMoreValuesError(PyTuple_GET_SIZE(t));
05969     } else {
05970       __Pyx_RaiseTooManyValuesError(index);
05971     }
05972 }
05973 
05974 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
05975 static int __Pyx_GetBuffer(PyObject *obj, Py_buffer *view, int flags) {
05976   #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02060000
05977   if (PyObject_CheckBuffer(obj)) return PyObject_GetBuffer(obj, view, flags);
05978   #endif
05979   if (PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, __pyx_ptype_5numpy_ndarray)) return __pyx_pf_5numpy_7ndarray___getbuffer__(obj, view, flags);
05980   else {
05981   PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError, "'%100s' does not have the buffer interface", Py_TYPE(obj)->tp_name);
05982   return -1;
05983     }
05984 }
05985 
05986 static void __Pyx_ReleaseBuffer(Py_buffer *view) {
05987   PyObject* obj = view->obj;
05988   if (obj) {
05989     #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02060000
05990     if (PyObject_CheckBuffer(obj)) {PyBuffer_Release(view); return;}
05991     #endif
05992     if (PyObject_TypeCheck(obj, __pyx_ptype_5numpy_ndarray)) __pyx_pf_5numpy_7ndarray_1__releasebuffer__(obj, view);
05993     Py_DECREF(obj);
05994     view->obj = NULL;
05995   }
05996 }

05999 
06000 static PyObject *__Pyx_Import(PyObject *name, PyObject *from_list, long level) {
06001     PyObject *py_import = 0;
06002     PyObject *empty_list = 0;
06003     PyObject *module = 0;
06004     PyObject *global_dict = 0;
06005     PyObject *empty_dict = 0;
06006     PyObject *list;
06007     py_import = __Pyx_GetAttrString(__pyx_b, "__import__");
06008     if (!py_import)
06009         goto bad;
06010     if (from_list)
06011         list = from_list;
06012     else {
06013         empty_list = PyList_New(0);
06014         if (!empty_list)
06015             goto bad;
06016         list = empty_list;
06017     }
06018     global_dict = PyModule_GetDict(__pyx_m);
06019     if (!global_dict)
06020         goto bad;
06021     empty_dict = PyDict_New();
06022     if (!empty_dict)
06023         goto bad;
06024     #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02050000
06025     {
06026         PyObject *py_level = PyInt_FromLong(level);
06027         if (!py_level)
06028             goto bad;
06029         module = PyObject_CallFunctionObjArgs(py_import,
06030             name, global_dict, empty_dict, list, py_level, NULL);
06031         Py_DECREF(py_level);
06032     }
06033     #else
06034     if (level>0) {
06035         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError, "Relative import is not supported for Python <=2.4.");
06036         goto bad;
06037     }
06038     module = PyObject_CallFunctionObjArgs(py_import,
06039         name, global_dict, empty_dict, list, NULL);
06040     #endif
06041 bad:
06042     Py_XDECREF(empty_list);
06043     Py_XDECREF(py_import);
06044     Py_XDECREF(empty_dict);
06045     return module;
06046 }
06047 
06048 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06049 static PyObject *__Pyx_GetStdout(void) {
06050     PyObject *f = PySys_GetObject((char *)"stdout");
06051     if (!f) {
06052         PyErr_SetString(PyExc_RuntimeError, "lost sys.stdout");
06053     }
06054     return f;
06055 }
06056 
06057 static int __Pyx_Print(PyObject* f, PyObject *arg_tuple, int newline) {
06058     PyObject* v;
06059     int i;
06060 
06061     if (!f) {
06062         if (!(f = __Pyx_GetStdout()))
06063             return -1;
06064     }
06065     for (i=0; i < PyTuple_GET_SIZE(arg_tuple); i++) {
06066         if (PyFile_SoftSpace(f, 1)) {
06067             if (PyFile_WriteString(" ", f) < 0)
06068                 return -1;
06069         }
06070         v = PyTuple_GET_ITEM(arg_tuple, i);
06071         if (PyFile_WriteObject(v, f, Py_PRINT_RAW) < 0)
06072             return -1;
06073         if (PyString_Check(v)) {
06074             char *s = PyString_AsString(v);
06075             Py_ssize_t len = PyString_Size(v);
06076             if (len > 0 &&
06077                 isspace(Py_CHARMASK(s[len-1])) &&
06078                 s[len-1] != ' ')
06079                     PyFile_SoftSpace(f, 0);
06080         }
06081     }
06082     if (newline) {
06083         if (PyFile_WriteString("\n", f) < 0)
06084             return -1;
06085         PyFile_SoftSpace(f, 0);
06086     }
06087     return 0;
06088 }
06089 
06090 #else /* Python 3 has a print function */
06091 
06092 static int __Pyx_Print(PyObject* stream, PyObject *arg_tuple, int newline) {
06093     PyObject* kwargs = 0;
06094     PyObject* result = 0;
06095     PyObject* end_string;
06096     if (unlikely(!__pyx_print)) {
06097         __pyx_print = __Pyx_GetAttrString(__pyx_b, "print");
06098         if (!__pyx_print)
06099             return -1;
06100     }
06101     if (stream) {
06102         kwargs = PyDict_New();
06103         if (unlikely(!kwargs))
06104             return -1;
06105         if (unlikely(PyDict_SetItemString(kwargs, "file", stream) < 0))
06106             goto bad;
06107         if (!newline) {
06108             end_string = PyUnicode_FromStringAndSize(" ", 1);
06109             if (unlikely(!end_string))
06110                 goto bad;
06111             if (PyDict_SetItemString(kwargs, "end", end_string) < 0) {
06112                 Py_DECREF(end_string);
06113                 goto bad;
06114             }
06115             Py_DECREF(end_string);
06116         }
06117     } else if (!newline) {
06118         if (unlikely(!__pyx_print_kwargs)) {
06119             __pyx_print_kwargs = PyDict_New();
06120             if (unlikely(!__pyx_print_kwargs))
06121                 return -1;
06122             end_string = PyUnicode_FromStringAndSize(" ", 1);
06123             if (unlikely(!end_string))
06124                 return -1;
06125             if (PyDict_SetItemString(__pyx_print_kwargs, "end", end_string) < 0) {
06126                 Py_DECREF(end_string);
06127                 return -1;
06128             }
06129             Py_DECREF(end_string);
06130         }
06131         kwargs = __pyx_print_kwargs;
06132     }
06133     result = PyObject_Call(__pyx_print, arg_tuple, kwargs);
06134     if (unlikely(kwargs) && (kwargs != __pyx_print_kwargs))
06135         Py_DECREF(kwargs);
06136     if (!result)
06137         return -1;
06138     Py_DECREF(result);
06139     return 0;
06140 bad:
06141     if (kwargs != __pyx_print_kwargs)
06142         Py_XDECREF(kwargs);
06143     return -1;
06144 }
06145 
06146 #endif
06147 
06148 #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06149 
06150 static int __Pyx_PrintOne(PyObject* f, PyObject *o) {
06151     if (!f) {
06152         if (!(f = __Pyx_GetStdout()))
06153             return -1;
06154     }
06155     if (PyFile_SoftSpace(f, 0)) {
06156         if (PyFile_WriteString(" ", f) < 0)
06157             return -1;
06158     }
06159     if (PyFile_WriteObject(o, f, Py_PRINT_RAW) < 0)
06160         return -1;
06161     if (PyFile_WriteString("\n", f) < 0)
06162         return -1;
06163     return 0;
06164     /* the line below is just to avoid compiler
06165      * compiler warnings about unused functions */
06166     return __Pyx_Print(f, NULL, 0);
06167 }
06168 
06169 #else /* Python 3 has a print function */
06170 
06171 static int __Pyx_PrintOne(PyObject* stream, PyObject *o) {
06172     int res;
06173     PyObject* arg_tuple = PyTuple_New(1);
06174     if (unlikely(!arg_tuple))
06175         return -1;
06176     Py_INCREF(o);
06177     PyTuple_SET_ITEM(arg_tuple, 0, o);
06178     res = __Pyx_Print(stream, arg_tuple, 1);
06179     Py_DECREF(arg_tuple);
06180     return res;
06181 }

06204 #if CYTHON_CCOMPLEX
06205 #else
06206     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_eqf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
06207        return (a.real == b.real) && (a.imag == b.imag);
06208     }
06209     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_sumf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
06210         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06211         z.real = a.real + b.real;
06212         z.imag = a.imag + b.imag;
06213         return z;
06214     }
06215     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_difff(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
06216         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06217         z.real = a.real - b.real;
06218         z.imag = a.imag - b.imag;
06219         return z;
06220     }
06221     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_prodf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
06222         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06223         z.real = a.real * b.real - a.imag * b.imag;
06224         z.imag = a.real * b.imag + a.imag * b.real;
06225         return z;
06226     }
06227     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_quotf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
06228         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06229         float denom = b.real * b.real + b.imag * b.imag;
06230         z.real = (a.real * b.real + a.imag * b.imag) / denom;
06231         z.imag = (a.imag * b.real - a.real * b.imag) / denom;
06232         return z;
06233     }
06234     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_negf(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
06235         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06236         z.real = -a.real;
06237         z.imag = -a.imag;
06238         return z;
06239     }
06240     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_is_zerof(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
06241        return (a.real == 0) && (a.imag == 0);
06242     }
06243     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_conjf(__pyx_t_float_complex a) {
06244         __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06245         z.real =  a.real;
06246         z.imag = -a.imag;
06247         return z;
06248     }
06249     #if 1
06250         static CYTHON_INLINE float __Pyx_c_absf(__pyx_t_float_complex z) {
06251           #if !defined(HAVE_HYPOT) || defined(_MSC_VER)
06252             return sqrtf(z.real*z.real + z.imag*z.imag);
06253           #else
06254             return hypotf(z.real, z.imag);
06255           #endif
06256         }
06257         static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_float_complex __Pyx_c_powf(__pyx_t_float_complex a, __pyx_t_float_complex b) {
06258             __pyx_t_float_complex z;
06259             float r, lnr, theta, z_r, z_theta;
06260             if (b.imag == 0 && b.real == (int)b.real) {
06261                 if (b.real < 0) {
06262                     float denom = a.real * a.real + a.imag * a.imag;
06263                     a.real = a.real / denom;
06264                     a.imag = -a.imag / denom;
06265                     b.real = -b.real;
06266                 }
06267                 switch ((int)b.real) {
06268                     case 0:
06269                         z.real = 1;
06270                         z.imag = 0;
06271                         return z;
06272                     case 1:
06273                         return a;
06274                     case 2:
06275                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
06276                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
06277                     case 3:
06278                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
06279                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(z, a);
06280                     case 4:
06281                         z = __Pyx_c_prodf(a, a);
06282                         return __Pyx_c_prodf(z, z);
06283                 }
06284             }
06285             if (a.imag == 0) {
06286                 if (a.real == 0) {
06287                     return a;
06288                 }
06289                 r = a.real;
06290                 theta = 0;
06291             } else {
06292                 r = __Pyx_c_absf(a);
06293                 theta = atan2f(a.imag, a.real);
06294             }
06295             lnr = logf(r);
06296             z_r = expf(lnr * b.real - theta * b.imag);
06297             z_theta = theta * b.real + lnr * b.imag;
06298             z.real = z_r * cosf(z_theta);
06299             z.imag = z_r * sinf(z_theta);
06300             return z;
06301         }
06302     #endif
06303 #endif

06327        return (a.real == b.real) && (a.imag == b.imag);
06328     }
06329     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_sum(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
06330         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06331         z.real = a.real + b.real;
06332         z.imag = a.imag + b.imag;
06333         return z;
06334     }
06335     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_diff(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
06336         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06337         z.real = a.real - b.real;
06338         z.imag = a.imag - b.imag;
06339         return z;
06340     }
06341     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_prod(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
06342         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06343         z.real = a.real * b.real - a.imag * b.imag;
06344         z.imag = a.real * b.imag + a.imag * b.real;
06345         return z;
06346     }
06347     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_quot(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
06348         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06349         double denom = b.real * b.real + b.imag * b.imag;
06350         z.real = (a.real * b.real + a.imag * b.imag) / denom;
06351         z.imag = (a.imag * b.real - a.real * b.imag) / denom;
06352         return z;
06353     }
06354     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_neg(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
06355         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06356         z.real = -a.real;
06357         z.imag = -a.imag;
06358         return z;
06359     }
06360     static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_c_is_zero(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
06361        return (a.real == 0) && (a.imag == 0);
06362     }
06363     static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_conj(__pyx_t_double_complex a) {
06364         __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06365         z.real =  a.real;
06366         z.imag = -a.imag;
06367         return z;
06368     }
06369     #if 1
06370         static CYTHON_INLINE double __Pyx_c_abs(__pyx_t_double_complex z) {
06371           #if !defined(HAVE_HYPOT) || defined(_MSC_VER)
06372             return sqrt(z.real*z.real + z.imag*z.imag);
06373           #else
06374             return hypot(z.real, z.imag);
06375           #endif
06376         }
06377         static CYTHON_INLINE __pyx_t_double_complex __Pyx_c_pow(__pyx_t_double_complex a, __pyx_t_double_complex b) {
06378             __pyx_t_double_complex z;
06379             double r, lnr, theta, z_r, z_theta;
06380             if (b.imag == 0 && b.real == (int)b.real) {
06381                 if (b.real < 0) {
06382                     double denom = a.real * a.real + a.imag * a.imag;
06383                     a.real = a.real / denom;
06384                     a.imag = -a.imag / denom;
06385                     b.real = -b.real;
06386                 }
06387                 switch ((int)b.real) {
06388                     case 0:
06389                         z.real = 1;
06390                         z.imag = 0;
06391                         return z;
06392                     case 1:
06393                         return a;
06394                     case 2:
06395                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
06396                         return __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
06397                     case 3:
06398                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
06399                         return __Pyx_c_prod(z, a);
06400                     case 4:
06401                         z = __Pyx_c_prod(a, a);
06402                         return __Pyx_c_prod(z, z);
06403                 }
06404             }
06405             if (a.imag == 0) {
06406                 if (a.real == 0) {
06407                     return a;
06408                 }
06409                 r = a.real;
06410                 theta = 0;
06411             } else {
06412                 r = __Pyx_c_abs(a);
06413                 theta = atan2(a.imag, a.real);
06414             }
06415             lnr = log(r);
06416             z_r = exp(lnr * b.real - theta * b.imag);
06417             z_theta = theta * b.real + lnr * b.imag;
06418             z.real = z_r * cos(z_theta);
06419             z.imag = z_r * sin(z_theta);
06420             return z;
06421         }
06422     #endif

06425 static CYTHON_INLINE unsigned char __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedChar(PyObject* x) {
06426     const unsigned char neg_one = (unsigned char)-1, const_zero = 0;
06427     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
06428     if (sizeof(unsigned char) < sizeof(long)) {
06429         long val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsLong(x);
06430         if (unlikely(val != (long)(unsigned char)val)) {
06431             if (!unlikely(val == -1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
06432                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
06433                     (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) ?
06434                     "can't convert negative value to unsigned char" :
06435                     "value too large to convert to unsigned char");
06436             }
06437             return (unsigned char)-1;
06438         }
06439         return (unsigned char)val;
06440     }
06441     return (unsigned char)__Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLong(x);
06442 }
06443

06501 static CYTHON_INLINE short __Pyx_PyInt_AsShort(PyObject* x) {
06502     const short neg_one = (short)-1, const_zero = 0;
06503     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
06504     if (sizeof(short) < sizeof(long)) {
06505         long val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsLong(x);
06506         if (unlikely(val != (long)(short)val)) {
06507             if (!unlikely(val == -1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
06508                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
06509                     (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) ?

06512             }
06513             return (short)-1;
06514         }
06515         return (short)val;
06516     }
06517     return (short)__Pyx_PyInt_AsLong(x);
06518 }
06519 
06520 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_PyInt_AsInt(PyObject* x) {
06521     const int neg_one = (int)-1, const_zero = 0;
06522     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
06523     if (sizeof(int) < sizeof(long)) {
06524         long val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsLong(x);
06525         if (unlikely(val != (long)(int)val)) {
06526             if (!unlikely(val == -1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
06527                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
06528                     (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) ?
06529                     "can't convert negative value to int" :
06530                     "value too large to convert to int");
06531             }
06532             return (int)-1;
06533         }
06534         return (int)val;
06535     }
06536     return (int)__Pyx_PyInt_AsLong(x);
06537 }
06538

06547                     (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) ?
06548                     "can't convert negative value to signed char" :
06549                     "value too large to convert to signed char");
06550             }
06551             return (signed char)-1;
06552         }

06615 static CYTHON_INLINE unsigned long __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLong(PyObject* x) {
06616     const unsigned long neg_one = (unsigned long)-1, const_zero = 0;
06617     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
06618 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
06619     if (likely(PyInt_Check(x))) {
06620         long val = PyInt_AS_LONG(x);
06621         if (is_unsigned && unlikely(val < 0)) {
06622             PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
06623                             "can't convert negative value to unsigned long");
06624             return (unsigned long)-1;
06625         }
06626         return (unsigned long)val;
06627     } else
06628 #endif
06629     if (likely(PyLong_Check(x))) {
06630         if (is_unsigned) {
06631             if (unlikely(Py_SIZE(x) < 0)) {
06632                 PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
06633                                 "can't convert negative value to unsigned long");
06634                 return (unsigned long)-1;
06635             }
06636             return (unsigned long)PyLong_AsUnsignedLong(x);
06637         } else {
06638             return (unsigned long)PyLong_AsLong(x);
06639         }
06640     } else {
06641         unsigned long val;
06642         PyObject *tmp = __Pyx_PyNumber_Int(x);
06643         if (!tmp) return (unsigned long)-1;
06644         val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLong(tmp);
06645         Py_DECREF(tmp);
06646         return val;
06647     }
06648 }
06649

06652     const int is_unsigned = neg_one > const_zero;
06653 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
06654     if (likely(PyInt_Check(x))) {

06671             return (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)PyLong_AsUnsignedLongLong(x);
06672         } else {

06825 static void __Pyx_WriteUnraisable(const char *name, int clineno,
06826                                   int lineno, const char *filename) {
06827     PyObject *old_exc, *old_val, *old_tb;
06828     PyObject *ctx;
06829     __Pyx_ErrFetch(&old_exc, &old_val, &old_tb);
06830     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06831     ctx = PyString_FromString(name);
06832     #else
06833     ctx = PyUnicode_FromString(name);
06834     #endif
06835     __Pyx_ErrRestore(old_exc, old_val, old_tb);
06836     if (!ctx) {
06837         PyErr_WriteUnraisable(Py_None);
06838     } else {
06839         PyErr_WriteUnraisable(ctx);
06840         Py_DECREF(ctx);
06841     }
06842 }
06843 
06844 static int __Pyx_check_binary_version(void) {
06845     char ctversion[4], rtversion[4];
06846     PyOS_snprintf(ctversion, 4, "%d.%d", PY_MAJOR_VERSION, PY_MINOR_VERSION);
06847     PyOS_snprintf(rtversion, 4, "%s", Py_GetVersion());
06848     if (ctversion[0] != rtversion[0] || ctversion[2] != rtversion[2]) {
06849         char message[200];
06850         PyOS_snprintf(message, sizeof(message),
06851                       "compiletime version %s of module '%.100s' "
06852                       "does not match runtime version %s",
06853                       ctversion, __Pyx_MODULE_NAME, rtversion);
06854         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
06855         return PyErr_Warn(NULL, message);
06856         #else
06857         return PyErr_WarnEx(NULL, message, 1);
06858         #endif
06859     }
06860     return 0;
06861 }
06862 
06863 static int __Pyx_SetVtable(PyObject *dict, void *vtable) {
06864 #if PY_VERSION_HEX >= 0x02070000 && !(PY_MAJOR_VERSION==3&&PY_MINOR_VERSION==0)
06865     PyObject *ob = PyCapsule_New(vtable, 0, 0);
06866 #else
06867     PyObject *ob = PyCObject_FromVoidPtr(vtable, 0);
06868 #endif
06869     if (!ob)
06870         goto bad;
06871     if (PyDict_SetItemString(dict, "__pyx_vtable__", ob) < 0)
06872         goto bad;
06873     Py_DECREF(ob);
06874     return 0;
06875 bad:
06876     Py_XDECREF(ob);
06877     return -1;
06878 }
06879 
06880 #ifndef __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportType
06881 #define __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportType
06882 static PyTypeObject *__Pyx_ImportType(const char *module_name, const char *class_name,
06883     size_t size, int strict)
06884 {
06885     PyObject *py_module = 0;
06886     PyObject *result = 0;
06887     PyObject *py_name = 0;
06888     char warning[200];
06889 
06890     py_module = __Pyx_ImportModule(module_name);
06891     if (!py_module)
06892         goto bad;
06893     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06894     py_name = PyString_FromString(class_name);
06895     #else
06896     py_name = PyUnicode_FromString(class_name);
06897     #endif
06898     if (!py_name)
06899         goto bad;
06900     result = PyObject_GetAttr(py_module, py_name);
06901     Py_DECREF(py_name);
06902     py_name = 0;
06903     Py_DECREF(py_module);
06904     py_module = 0;
06905     if (!result)
06906         goto bad;
06907     if (!PyType_Check(result)) {
06908         PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
06909             "%s.%s is not a type object",
06910             module_name, class_name);
06911         goto bad;
06912     }
06913     if (!strict && ((PyTypeObject *)result)->tp_basicsize > (Py_ssize_t)size) {
06914         PyOS_snprintf(warning, sizeof(warning),
06915             "%s.%s size changed, may indicate binary incompatibility",
06916             module_name, class_name);
06917         #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
06918         if (PyErr_Warn(NULL, warning) < 0) goto bad;
06919         #else
06920         if (PyErr_WarnEx(NULL, warning, 0) < 0) goto bad;
06921         #endif
06922     }
06923     else if (((PyTypeObject *)result)->tp_basicsize != (Py_ssize_t)size) {
06924         PyErr_Format(PyExc_ValueError,
06925             "%s.%s has the wrong size, try recompiling",
06926             module_name, class_name);
06927         goto bad;
06928     }
06929     return (PyTypeObject *)result;
06930 bad:
06931     Py_XDECREF(py_module);
06932     Py_XDECREF(result);
06933     return NULL;
06934 }
06935 #endif
06936 
06937 #ifndef __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportModule
06938 #define __PYX_HAVE_RT_ImportModule
06939 static PyObject *__Pyx_ImportModule(const char *name) {
06940     PyObject *py_name = 0;
06941     PyObject *py_module = 0;
06942 
06943     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06944     py_name = PyString_FromString(name);
06945     #else
06946     py_name = PyUnicode_FromString(name);
06947     #endif
06948     if (!py_name)
06949         goto bad;
06950     py_module = PyImport_Import(py_name);
06951     Py_DECREF(py_name);
06952     return py_module;
06953 bad:
06954     Py_XDECREF(py_name);
06955     return 0;
06956 }
06957 #endif
06958 
06959 #include "compile.h"
06960 #include "frameobject.h"
06961 #include "traceback.h"
06962 
06963 static void __Pyx_AddTraceback(const char *funcname, int __pyx_clineno,
06964                                int __pyx_lineno, const char *__pyx_filename) {
06965     PyObject *py_srcfile = 0;
06966     PyObject *py_funcname = 0;
06967     PyObject *py_globals = 0;
06968     PyCodeObject *py_code = 0;
06969     PyFrameObject *py_frame = 0;
06970 
06971     #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06972     py_srcfile = PyString_FromString(__pyx_filename);
06973     #else
06974     py_srcfile = PyUnicode_FromString(__pyx_filename);
06975     #endif
06976     if (!py_srcfile) goto bad;
06977     if (__pyx_clineno) {
06978         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06979         py_funcname = PyString_FromFormat( "%s (%s:%d)", funcname, __pyx_cfilenm, __pyx_clineno);
06980         #else
06981         py_funcname = PyUnicode_FromFormat( "%s (%s:%d)", funcname, __pyx_cfilenm, __pyx_clineno);
06982         #endif
06983     }
06984     else {
06985         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
06986         py_funcname = PyString_FromString(funcname);
06987         #else
06988         py_funcname = PyUnicode_FromString(funcname);
06989         #endif
06990     }
06991     if (!py_funcname) goto bad;
06992     py_globals = PyModule_GetDict(__pyx_m);
06993     if (!py_globals) goto bad;
06994     py_code = PyCode_New(
06995         0,            /*int argcount,*/
06996         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION >= 3
06997         0,            /*int kwonlyargcount,*/
06998         #endif
06999         0,            /*int nlocals,*/
07000         0,            /*int stacksize,*/
07001         0,            /*int flags,*/
07002         __pyx_empty_bytes, /*PyObject *code,*/
07003         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *consts,*/
07004         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *names,*/
07005         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *varnames,*/
07006         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *freevars,*/
07007         __pyx_empty_tuple,  /*PyObject *cellvars,*/
07008         py_srcfile,   /*PyObject *filename,*/
07009         py_funcname,  /*PyObject *name,*/
07010         __pyx_lineno,   /*int firstlineno,*/
07011         __pyx_empty_bytes  /*PyObject *lnotab*/
07012     );
07013     if (!py_code) goto bad;
07014     py_frame = PyFrame_New(
07015         PyThreadState_GET(), /*PyThreadState *tstate,*/
07016         py_code,             /*PyCodeObject *code,*/
07017         py_globals,          /*PyObject *globals,*/
07018         0                    /*PyObject *locals*/
07019     );
07020     if (!py_frame) goto bad;
07021     py_frame->f_lineno = __pyx_lineno;
07022     PyTraceBack_Here(py_frame);
07023 bad:
07024     Py_XDECREF(py_srcfile);
07025     Py_XDECREF(py_funcname);
07026     Py_XDECREF(py_code);
07027     Py_XDECREF(py_frame);
07028 }
07029 
07030 static int __Pyx_InitStrings(__Pyx_StringTabEntry *t) {
07031     while (t->p) {
07032         #if PY_MAJOR_VERSION < 3
07033         if (t->is_unicode) {
07034             *t->p = PyUnicode_DecodeUTF8(t->s, t->n - 1, NULL);
07035         } else if (t->intern) {
07036             *t->p = PyString_InternFromString(t->s);
07037         } else {
07038             *t->p = PyString_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
07039         }
07040         #else  /* Python 3+ has unicode identifiers */
07041         if (t->is_unicode | t->is_str) {
07042             if (t->intern) {
07043                 *t->p = PyUnicode_InternFromString(t->s);
07044             } else if (t->encoding) {
07045                 *t->p = PyUnicode_Decode(t->s, t->n - 1, t->encoding, NULL);
07046             } else {
07047                 *t->p = PyUnicode_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
07048             }
07049         } else {
07050             *t->p = PyBytes_FromStringAndSize(t->s, t->n - 1);
07051         }
07052         #endif
07053         if (!*t->p)
07054             return -1;
07055         ++t;
07056     }
07057     return 0;
07058 }
07059 
07060 /* Type Conversion Functions */
07061 
07062 static CYTHON_INLINE int __Pyx_PyObject_IsTrue(PyObject* x) {
07063    int is_true = x == Py_True;
07064    if (is_true | (x == Py_False) | (x == Py_None)) return is_true;
07065    else return PyObject_IsTrue(x);
07066 }
07067 
07068 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject* __Pyx_PyNumber_Int(PyObject* x) {
07069   PyNumberMethods *m;
07070   const char *name = NULL;
07071   PyObject *res = NULL;
07072 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
07073   if (PyInt_Check(x) || PyLong_Check(x))
07074 #else
07075   if (PyLong_Check(x))
07076 #endif
07077     return Py_INCREF(x), x;
07078   m = Py_TYPE(x)->tp_as_number;
07079 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
07080   if (m && m->nb_int) {
07081     name = "int";
07082     res = PyNumber_Int(x);
07083   }
07084   else if (m && m->nb_long) {
07085     name = "long";
07086     res = PyNumber_Long(x);
07087   }
07088 #else
07089   if (m && m->nb_int) {
07090     name = "int";
07091     res = PyNumber_Long(x);
07092   }
07093 #endif
07094   if (res) {
07095 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x03000000
07096     if (!PyInt_Check(res) && !PyLong_Check(res)) {
07097 #else
07098     if (!PyLong_Check(res)) {
07099 #endif
07100       PyErr_Format(PyExc_TypeError,
07101                    "__%s__ returned non-%s (type %.200s)",
07102                    name, name, Py_TYPE(res)->tp_name);
07103       Py_DECREF(res);
07104       return NULL;
07105     }
07106   }
07107   else if (!PyErr_Occurred()) {
07108     PyErr_SetString(PyExc_TypeError,
07109                     "an integer is required");
07110   }
07111   return res;
07112 }
07113 
07114 static CYTHON_INLINE Py_ssize_t __Pyx_PyIndex_AsSsize_t(PyObject* b) {
07115   Py_ssize_t ival;
07116   PyObject* x = PyNumber_Index(b);
07117   if (!x) return -1;
07118   ival = PyInt_AsSsize_t(x);
07119   Py_DECREF(x);
07120   return ival;
07121 }
07122 
07123 static CYTHON_INLINE PyObject * __Pyx_PyInt_FromSize_t(size_t ival) {
07124 #if PY_VERSION_HEX < 0x02050000
07125    if (ival <= LONG_MAX)
07126        return PyInt_FromLong((long)ival);
07127    else {
07128        unsigned char *bytes = (unsigned char *) &ival;
07129        int one = 1; int little = (int)*(unsigned char*)&one;
07130        return _PyLong_FromByteArray(bytes, sizeof(size_t), little, 0);
07131    }
07132 #else
07133    return PyInt_FromSize_t(ival);
07134 #endif
07135 }
07136 
07137 static CYTHON_INLINE size_t __Pyx_PyInt_AsSize_t(PyObject* x) {
07138    unsigned PY_LONG_LONG val = __Pyx_PyInt_AsUnsignedLongLong(x);
07139    if (unlikely(val == (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)-1 && PyErr_Occurred())) {
07140        return (size_t)-1;
07141    } else if (unlikely(val != (unsigned PY_LONG_LONG)(size_t)val)) {
07142        PyErr_SetString(PyExc_OverflowError,
07143                        "value too large to convert to size_t");
07144        return (size_t)-1;
07145    }
07146    return (size_t)val;
07147 }
